 He said that thousands of papers are used daily in the Supreme Court and this will also benefit the environment
 muvvakil ko pataa rahegaa ki kya date he sunwaayee kii, kya kharch aayaa
 The biggest advantage is that if a case is filed against a government department, then at the time of filing, the department will know that a case has been filed against it
 isse wo puure cese file ko downlod kar saktaa he
 Justice Khehar said that i took office on January 4 this year and within a week i got a letter from the Law Minister that the government has given Rs 438 crore but after three sessions it was found that only 20% of the fund has been spent
 mujhe pataa tha ki court main soochna or takanic ke saath saath computerisenation main sarkaar hamaari madad karne ko taiyaar he
 The database has grown and now the Supreme Court is ready to be paperless
 justise khehar ne kaha ki 6 maheene pehle justise e em khanalevkar ne bataaya ki unke dimag main ek safteware he jis par kaam ho saktaa he

 supreme court ab tak baari bharkam kagaji kaam hota he

 ) More than a million people have signed a petition demanding a second referendum in this regard after Britain voted in favor of quitting EU membership
 yachika parabritish sansadamein charchaa hogi
 1,00,000 signatures are required to debate an issue in the UK House of Commons
 guruuvar ko huejanmat sangrahame desh ke 52 pratishat logon ne europea sangh kii sadsyta chhodane (live) ke paksh main jabaki 48 pratishat logon ne isamen bane rahane (remean) ke paksh main matdaan kiya
 However, London, Scotland and Northern Ireland had more voting in favor of remaining in the European Union, with the remainder voting more in favor of leaving membership
 kul 72 pratishat logon ne matdaan kiya
 The number of people who signed the petition reached one million on Sunday morning
 inamen se zyaadaatar hastakshar landan, brighaton, oxford, cambridge or manchester ke logon ne kiye
 The petition, initiated by William Oliver Heale, said, 'we demand the British government to enforce a rule under the signature campaign that if the Remain or Leave vote is less than 60 per cent, with a turnout of less than 75 per cent
 And there should be a referendum
 â€™ duusare janamat sangrah ke liye baari sankhya main logon ke hastakshar karne kii vajah se ek samay sansadeey yachika kii website krash ho gai
 It is unclear whether this will be implemented from the previous date or whether it will be introduced into British law after the demand for changes in the rules
 akhil bhartiya ayurvigyaan santhaan (ames) ke sutron ne ravivaar ko kaha ki sunanda pushkar ke sharir main sharaab ke ansh nahin paae gaye, lekin unhone depressant kii dawa kaa overdoj liya tha
 The post-mortem of Sunanda's body was performed by a three-member board of doctors at AIIMS on Saturday
 doctoron ne kaha tha ki sunanda kii maut 'achaanak or aswabhaavik' he
 AIIMS sources said on Sunday that doctors have not found any alcohol content in the body, but the possibility of the presence of alprazolam, a drug used in mental distress, cannot be ruled out
 jaanchakartaaon ko hotel ke kamare se alprax kii khaali pattee mili thi
 It was feared in media reports that a combination of alcohol and anti-depressants would have caused the death

 ) New Delhi Municipal Council (NDMC) is going to start a taxi service with women drivers to protect women in Delhi

 Millions of women in the world suffer from urinary tract infection (UTI) due to retention of urine for several hours

 in logon ke paas paanch sau hazaar kii sankhya main bill hote hai, jisaki soochna bharte bharte kai ghante lag jate hai
 Previously, the merchant used to pay CA for a full year Rs 1500, now he has to pay twenty to twenty five thousand rupees for the whole year
 jiesti ne laghu va madhyam shrenee ke bijnesaman or udhyamiyon ko pareshaan kar diya he
 The question has arisen whether they will survive in the market or not
 hamane ek sawaal poocha ki aakhri din vyapaaree kyon bharte hai to iskaa jawaab yun mila Then you tell me why these last dates are kept
 aapkaa system last date ke hisaab se taiyaar kyon nahin he
 Should the merchant leave all the work and get the returns filled? Can not all traders fill GST by themselves? tex conslatent se baat karne par pataa chalaa ki chote shaharon main sthiti or bhi karaab he
 Internet does not work, but it runs slow
 ofline form bharkar jab aap online main migrat karaate hai to kai baar system sweekaar nahin karata he
 The condition is that there are 250 clients, but even after three to four days GST of 50% could not be filled
 rifund kii samasya vyapaaree khub uthaa rahe hai
 They are saying that when July refunds will be received after November 10, then august-september and October refunds will be available after March next year
 is kaaran vyapaariyon ke haath main paisa hi nahin he
 Payment is stuck at every level
 jinhone bank se lone liye hai, wo baad main alag se byaaz bhi bharenge
 We spoke to an officer of the All India Transport Association, listing what they told us
 jiesti ke aane ke baad se transport sector kii haalat or karaab ho gai he
 In July, the turnover had come down to 20 percent, in August it came to 50 percent
 sitambar main 60 fisadi tak pahunchaa he magar ab bhi 30-40 fisadi bijness down he
 There has not been a significant difference in the timing of the trucks' rounds as the octroi had moved everywhere except Maharashtra
 dilli mumbai root par zarur trek ke pahunchane ke samay main das ghante kii kami ai he
 There are several reasons for this
 abhi bhi badi sankhya main vyapaariyon kaa registration nahin hua he
 Without registration the transporter cannot pick up their cargo because it will be caught
 nayaa niyam aisa hi he
 Still, the goods of those who have not been registered are going from here to there
 kaise ho rahaa he
 It is happening that the transporters taking the risk for this are charging twice as much
 is vakt sarkaar checking karne kii sthiti main nahin he
 But a large number of transporters want only the registered merchants to pick up the goods, but the business of those who have registered has reduced by 40 to 50 percent
 unke paas se transporter ko order nahin mil rahaa he
 Therefore trucks in warehouses are standing in large numbers which is not a good sign for any business or economy
 bijness down hone kaa trakon par or asar padaa he
 For example, trucks from Delhi which have gone south due to freight, are stuck there
 kyonki vahaan kii factriyon main utpaadan down he, trakon ko maal nahin mil rahaa he
 Therefore, instead of returning, they have been stuck in the cities of the south for a week
 transporter ne bataaya ki kam se kam 1000 se lekar 2000 tak trek dilli ke vahaan atake honge
 This never happened in the Diwali season
 ye sirf trek kii baat he, agar aap isamen transport main istamaal hone vaali trailor,chote trek, tampo ko bhi shaamil karenge to tasviir kuch or nazar aegi
 We have written all these things on the basis of conversation so that we know what is happening on the ground
 kisi bhi vyapaaree ne nahin kaha ki ve tex nahin dena chaahate
 Everyone wants to give but is very upset with the process and the rate of taxes
 maine rajasthan ke kuch vyapaar sanghon ke pratinidhiyon se phone par baat kii
 The business of marble, handi craft and gold jewelery is very important in Rajasthan
 pehle donon par 28 fisadi jiesti lagi he or gold jewelri par 3 fisadi jiesti lagi he
 Sitaram Agarwal Saheb of Steel Association said that our business has been down by 40%
 tiamati saria, angel, panel in sab kii bikri bahut hi kam rah gai he
 In factories where three shifts were going on, there are two shifts
 over time karne vaale kii kamai kam ho gai kyonki over time band he yaa kam he
 Daily laborers are not getting work in every sector, this is the most affected
 vaise bhi bainkon ke en pi e main 39 fisadi hissaa steel sector kaa hi he
 In Rajasthan, the consumption of petrol and diesel has come down by six and a half percent
 ham sarkaar ko positive suzav dete hai, magar koi ection nahin hota
 The diagnosis of problems at the local level has stopped
 isi tarah hamane jaipur ke pattharon ko taraash kar fansy item banane vaale ek kaarobaari se baat hui
 On the condition of anonymity, he said that his business has fallen by 80 percent
 28 fisadi jiesti ke kaaran chizein itani mahangi ho gayi ki logon ne shaukia kareed band kar di
 The business of the first month was from fifty to six lakhs, which has now come down to ten to 15 lakhs
 iskaa asar rojgaar par padaa he
 They told that hamaari factory main jo mahange or sthaayee acountint the unako hataanaa padaa

 teen teen kantrector the, harek ke paas 10 se 15 mazdoor kaam kar rahe the

 magar ab kisi kantrector ke paas do se teen mazaduron se zyada kaa kaam nahin he yani har kisi ke 10 se 12 mazaduron se kaam chhin gaya he

 ek pranali or teen tex vaali jiesti ke aagaman kaa swaagat 15 agast 1947 kii madhyaraatri kii tarah kiya gaya, jiesti ke kaaran jinke pet par chot padi he, kya unhen bulaakar sansad main sammanit nahin karnaa chahie
 Last time in prime time when we were talking about bank strike, a voice was heard saying that jobs in banking sector have reduced
 aam taur par is saal tak bank bhartiyon ke liye ai bi pi es ko bataa detii he,institute aaf banking personal salection naam kii yah sanstha bank sevaaon main bhartiyon ke liye pariksha yojit karti he
 Let's look at the data found from the IBPS website
 2015 main 24, 604 clerkon kii bhartee kaa vigyaapan niklaa tha
 In 2016, an advertisement for the recruitment of 19,243 clerks came out
 ek saal main clerkon kii bhartee main 5,361 kii kami aa gai
 The recruitment of 7,883 clerks is vacant in 2017
 2016 se 17 ke bich 11,360 pad kam ho gaye
 Compared to 2015, 16,000 vacancies have decreased
 noujvaan aaj berojgaare ke registan main khadaa he or aapkaa netaa kabristaan kii baat kar rahaa he
 It cannot be said more clearly than this
 ab aate hai probationar afisar pio kii sankhya par
 The story here is also sad
 2015 main 12,434 post pio kaa niklaa tha
 In 2016, the direct 3612 was reduced to 8,822
 2017 main 3,562 pio kii hi vaikency nikali he
 That is, there are about 9000 less vacancies in 2017 as compared to 2015
 aaj ke hi indian express pradhanmantri kaushal vikaas yojana par ek report chhapi he
 You will also read the reports of Anchal Magazine and Anil Sasi

 usee se pataa chalata he ki kyon media rojgaar kii baat nahin karata, kyon hindu muslim taapic kii baat karata he

 par kya quality itani ausat thi ki 30 lakh main se teen lakh ko bhi rojgaar nahin mila to phir is yojana ke tahat thik kya tha
 Isn't this figure intimidating, would you still like to leave a worry about the future of the youth and see the debate on Hindu Muslim topics
 karnaa kya he, naujavaanon ko dangai bananaa he yaa naagarik bananaa he
 There is no reliable and transparent data system for employment in our country
 itani chizon ke ap banate hai, ek ap isi kaa ban jaataa jisase yahi pataa chalata ki is maheene centre ke kis vibhaag ne yaa rajya sarkaron ke kis vibhaag ne naukariyaan nikaali hai
 But governments will not tell because you will know the reality
 susheel mahapatra kii report dekhie, jiesti ke asar par kya kehete hai ricycling factory vaale
 Even after September 20 in Jaipur, the portal was not functioning properly
 puure din massej aate rahaa ki aap qataar main he, din biit gaya qataar nahin beetaa

 acha hota masik kii jagah tremasik ritern bharne kii vyavastha hoti
 The port is in English only, due to which traders are unable to understand or fill it
 galati se batan sabamit ho gaya to sudhaar karne kii koi guzaaish nahin he
 For example, if any amount is deposited in some other item, then it is not getting a chance to improve
 sarkaar kahati hi 3 bi farm bharne kii deree par jurmaana nahin lagegaa, magar liya ja rahaa he
 There is a fine of 200 rupees for one day delay
 aksar portal ke kaaran farm bharne main deree ho rahi he, tab bhi jurmaana lag rahaa he
 The assumption is not correct that CA and tax lawyers are having fun for this reason, but the fact is that they are also very upset
 vyapaariyon kii pareshaani to or bhi badi he

 ve bazaar main tikenge yaa nahin, ye sawaal khadaa ho gaya he

 har level par pement atka hua he

 july main to ghandha ghatakar 20 fisadi par aa gaya tha, agast main 50 fisadi tak aayaa

 iske kai kaaran he

 bina registration ke transporter unka maal nahin uthaa saktaa kyonki pakadaa jayega
 The New Testament is like this
 phir bhi jinhone registration nahin karaayaa he, unka maal yahaan se vahaan ja to rahaa he

 lekin bahut badi sankhya main transporter chaahate hai ki registration vaale vyapaaree kaa hi maal uthaaen, magar jin logon ne registration karaayaa he unka bijness 40 se 50 fisadi kam ho gaya he
 The transporter is not getting orders from them
 isliye godaamon main trek badi sankhya main khaali khadey hai jo kisi bijness yaa arthvyavastha ke liye shubh sanket nahin he

 jaise dilli se jo trek maal kar dakshin kii taraf gaye hai, vahaan jaakar atak gaye hai

 isliye vaapasi kii jagah ve hafte bhar se dakshin ke shaharon main atake hai

 diwali ke sizan main aisa kabhi nahin hota tha

 Now it is being thought that the quality of training is not average
 par kya quality itani ausat thi ki 30 lakh main se teen lakh ko bhi rojgaar nahin mila to phir is yojana ke tahat thik kya tha
 Isn't this figure intimidating, would you still like to leave a worry about the future of the youth and see the debate on Hindu Muslim topics
 karnaa kya he, naujavaanon ko dangai bananaa he yaa naagarik bananaa he
 There is no reliable and transparent data system for employment in our country
 itani chizon ke ap banate hai, ek ap isi kaa ban jaataa jisase yahi pataa chalata ki is maheene centre ke kis vibhaag ne yaa rajya sarkaron ke kis vibhaag ne naukariyaan nikaali hai
 But governments will not tell because you will know the reality
 susheel mahapatra kii report dekhie, jiesti ke asar par kya kehete hai ricycling factory vaale
 The condition of the transport sector has worsened since the introduction of GST
 july main to ghandha ghatakar 20 fisadi par aa gaya tha, agast main 50 fisadi tak aayaa
 60 percent reached in September but still 30-40 percent business down
 trakon ke phere ke samay main bhi khaas antar nahin aayaa he kyonki maharashtra ko chhod oktry har jagah se hat gaya tha
 The arrival time of the truck on the Delhi Mumbai route has reduced by ten hours
 iske kai kaaran he
 Still a large number of traders have not been registered
 bina registration ke transporter unka maal nahin uthaa saktaa kyonki pakadaa jayega
 The New Testament is like this
 phir bhi jinhone registration nahin karaayaa he, unka maal yahaan se vahaan ja to rahaa he
 How is it happening aise ho rahaa he ki iske liye jokhim uthaane vaale transporter dugana tiguna charge kar rahe hai
 At this time the government is not in a position to check
 lekin bahut badi sankhya main transporter chaahate hai ki registration vaale vyapaaree kaa hi maal uthaaen, magar jin logon ne registration karaayaa he unka bijness 40 se 50 fisadi kam ho gaya he
 The transporter is not getting orders from them
 isliye godaamon main trek badi sankhya main khaali khadey hai jo kisi bijness yaa arthvyavastha ke liye shubh sanket nahin he
 The downsizing of trucks has further impacted the trucks
 jaise dilli se jo trek maal kar dakshin kii taraf gaye hai, vahaan jaakar atak gaye hai
 Because the factories there are down production, trucks are not getting the goods
 isliye vaapasi kii jagah ve hafte bhar se dakshin ke shaharon main atake hai
 The transporter said that at least 1000 to 2000 trucks will be stuck in Delhi
 diwali ke sizan main aisa kabhi nahin hota tha
 This is just a matter of truck, if you include the trailer, small truck, tampo used in transport, then the picture will look something else
 hamane ye sabhi baaten baatcheet ke aadhaar par likhi hai jisase pataa chale ki zamin par kya ho rahaa he
 None of the traders said that they do not want to pay tax
 sab dena chaahate hai magar prakriya or karon kii dar se kaaphi pareshaan hai
 i spoke to representatives of some trade associations in Rajasthan over the phone
 rajasthan main marble, handi craft or gold jewelri kaa kaarobaar kaaphi ahm rakhata he
 The first has a GST of 28 per cent on both and 3 per cent GST on gold jewelery
 steel sangh ke seetaram agarwal sahab ne kaha ki hamaara bijness 40 percent down ho gaya he
 Sales of TMT bars, angles, panels have all been very low
 factriyon main jahaan teen shift chal rahi thi vahaan do shift chal rahi he
 The overtime earns less because the overtime is closed or less
 har sector main dihadi mazaduron ko kaam nahin mil rahaa he, sabase prabhavit yahi he
 As such, the steel sector accounts for 39 per cent of the banks' npas
 rajasthan main petrol or deazal kii khapat main saadhe chah fisadi kii kami aa gai he
 We give positive suggestions to the government, but there is no action
 sthaneey str par samasyaon kaa nidaan to band hi ho gaya he
 Similarly we talked to a businessman who made fancy items by carving stones from Jaipur
 naam na bataane kii shart par kaha ki unke bijness main 80 fisadi kii giravat ai he
 Due to 28 per cent GST, things became so expensive that people stopped buying amateur
 pehle maheene kaa bijness pachaas se saath lakh kaa hota tha jo ab ghatakar das se 15 lakh par aa gaya he
 This has impacted employment
 unhone bataaya ki Those who were expensive and permanent accountants in our factory had to be removed
 aise kai logon kii chantni kii or unki jagah part time kaam liya
 There were three contractors, each with 10 to 15 laborers working
 pehle maheene hi do kantrector ko waapas bhej diya, ab bulaayaa he
 But now no contractor has more than two to three laborers, ie 10 to 12 laborers have been lost
 ham jiesti kii samasya ko portal tak hi simit na rakhen, iske kaaran vyapaar jo manda padaa he or dihadi par kamaane waalon ke haath se jo kaam chhina he, uskaa koi hisaab nahin he
 The arrival of a system and a three-taxed GST was welcomed like the midnight of 15 August 1947, due to the GST, those who have suffered injuries on their stomachs should not be called and honored in Parliament
 pichhali baar prime time main jab ham bank hadtaal par baat kar rahe the to ek awaz sunai di ki banking sector main naukariyaan kam ho gai hai
 Normally till this year the bank informs IBPS for the recruitment, this institution called Institute of Banking Personal Selection conducts the examination for the recruitment in the bank services
 ai bi pi es kii website se jo data mila he, use dekhte hai
 In 2015, advertisements for recruitment of 24, 604 clerks were released
 2016 main 19, 243 clerkon kii bhartee kaa vigyaapan niklaa
 The recruitment of clerks decreased by 5,361 in one year
 2017 main 7,883 clerkon kii bhartee kii vekainsee ai he
 Between 2016 and 17, 11,360 posts were reduced
 2015 kii tulana main saulah hazaar vaikency kam ho gai he
 The young man stands in the desert of unemployment today and your leader is talking about the graveyard
 isse saaf saaf or isse zyaada kuch nahin kah saktaa
 Now comes the number of Probationer Officer P
O
 yahaan bhi kahani dukhad he
 In 2015, there were 12,434 posts of pos
 2016 main sidhaa 3612 kam ho kar 8,822 ho gaya
 In 2017, only 3,562 PO vacancies have come out
 yani 2015 kii tulana main 2017 main kareeb 9000 kam vekainsee ai he
 Today's Indian Express has published a report on Pradhan Mantri Kaushal Vikas Yojana
 anchal magazine or anil sasi kii report aap bhi padhiyegaa
 The Ministry of Skill Development is reviewing demand and supply at the district level, collecting data
 july 2017 ke pehle hafte tak ke data ko dekhne ke baad jo tasviir saamne aa rahi he wo bhayaavah he
 The same shows why the media does not talk about employment, why Hindu talks about Muslim topics
 express kii is report main likhaa he kitippaniyan So far, under the skill development scheme, 30 lakh 67 thousand people have been trained or were being given
 inamen se maatr 2 lakh 90 hazaar ko hi kaam mila he
 There is a target of training one crore youth in four years under this scheme of 12,000 crores
 ab ye chintan ho rahaa he ki kahin training kii quality to ausat nahin he
 But was the quality so average that even out of 30 lakh three lakhs did not get employment, then what was right under this scheme? kya yah aankada daraane vaala nahin he, kya ab bhi aap naujavaanon ke bhavishya kii chintaa chhodkar hindu muslim taapic par bahes dekhnaa chahenge
 What to do, whether to riot the youth or to make them citizens
 hamaare desh main rojgaar ko lekar koi vishwasaneey or paardarshee data system nahin he
 App for so many things are made, an app would be made by it, which shows that this month which department of the center or which department of state governments have taken out jobs

 ham sarkaar ko positive suzav dete hai, magar koi ection nahin hota

 isi tarah hamane jaipur ke pattharon ko taraash kar fansy item banane vaale ek kaarobaari se baat hui

 Neem has anti-fungal, anti-bacterial and anti-inflammatory properties
 ye lagbhag har tarah ke infections ko dur karne kaa ek behad kargar or natural upaay he
 While neem stalk is used as a toothpick, its bark is used to remove ringworm and other infections
 isaki pattiyon kaa istemaal skin se judi kai samasyaon main kiya jaataa he
 In addition, they are also very effective in treating smallpox
 ye chechak ko badhane se rokane kaa kaam karti hai
 By applying neem on the victim's body and other measures, we can reduce its infection
 chechak ho jane par neem ke in upayon ko karnaa rahegaa phydemand:1
 After pox, bathing with neem leaves will be very beneficial
 aap chaahe to neem kii pattiyon ko ek gahare bartan main dhakkar ubaal sakate hai
 When this water cools down, filter it

 Apart from this, if you want, put neem leaves in lukewarm water and leave it for some time
 10 se 15 minute tak ise yun hi rahane den
 Bathe the patient with this water

 Chickenpox is an infectious disease that can occur from one person to another

 bistar par neem kii pattiyon ko failaa den
 It will give relief and control itching

 Indian Space Agency ISRO has described the difficulties of the Chandrayaan-2 mission
 isamen bataaya gaya he ki bhartiya vaigyanik chandrayan-2 ko launch karne ke baad use chand par land karaane tak kis tarah kii samasyaon se rubaru hone vaale hai
 However, scientists have expressed confidence that they will meet all these challenges
 chandrayan-2 ko 9 se 16 july ke bich choda jayega
 Seven challenges will come in front of the first challenge in the journey of Chandrayaan-2: The distance of the moon from the Earth will be about 3 lakh 84 thousand 400 km at the time of taking the right path
 itane lambey safar ke liye sabase jaruri sahi maarg (tregectory) kaa chunaav karnaa
 Because with the right trajectory, Chandrayaan-2 will have less impact on the gravity of the earth, moon and other objects coming in the way, solar radiation and the movement of the moon
 duusari chunauteeh gahare antariksh main sanchardharti se zyada duuri hone kii vajah se radio signal deree se pahunchenge
 Delayed reply
 saath hi antariksh main hone vaali aawaaj bhi sanchaar main baadha pahuchaanenge
 Third challenge: Reaching the moon's orbit Chandrayaan-2 will not be easy to reach the moon's orbit
 lagaataar badalte orbital movement kii vajah se chandrayan-2 ko chand kii kaksha main pahunchane ke liye atyadhik sateekta kii jarurat hogi
 It will cost a lot of fuel
 sahi kaksha main pahunchane par hi tay jagah par landing ho paaegi
 Fourth challenge: Walking in the moon's orbit It will not be easy for Chandrayaan-2 to revolve around the moon
 iskaa bada kaaran he chand ke chaaron taraf gravity baraabar nahin he
 This affects the electronics of Chandrayaan-2
 isliye, chand kii gravity or vaataavaran kii bhi baariki se gananaa kerani hogi
 Fifth Challenge: Soft Landing on the Moon According to ISRO scientists, the biggest challenge is the soft landing of the rover and lander on the Moon to Chandrayaan-2
 chand kii kaksha se dakshini dhruv par rover or lander ko aaraam se utaarne ke liye propalshan system or onboard computer kaa kaam mukhya hoga
 All these works will be done automatically
 chhathin chunauteeh chandramaa kii dhulchand kii sataha par dheron gadde, pathar or dhul he
 As soon as the lander turns on its propulsion system on the lunar surface, there will be rapid dust blowing
 dhul udakar lander ke solar panel par jamaa ho sakati he, isse power supplai baadhit ho sakati he
 Onboard computer sensors may be affected
 saatvin chunauteeh badalata tapamaanachaand kaa ek din yaa raat dharti ke 14 din ke baraabar hoti he
 Because of this, the temperature on the lunar surface changes rapidly
 isse lander or rover ke kaam main baadha aegi

 After 11 years, the Indian Space Agency ISRO is ready to explore the lunar surface once again
 dakshini dhruv ke paas utrega chandrayan-2isro ne ummid jataai he ki chandrayan-2 chandramaa par 6 sitambar ko dakshini dhruv ke paas utrega
 Chandrayaan-2 has three parts, named Orbiter, Lander (vikram) and Rover (pragya)
 is project kii laagat 800 karod rupye he
 Between 9 and 16 July, the distance of the Moon from Earth will be 384400 kilometers
 agar mishan safal hua to america, rus, china ke baad bharat chand par rover utaarne vaala chauthaa desh hoga
 The most powerful rocket will be launched from GSLV Mark-3, Chandrayaan-2 will be released outside the Earth's orbit from isro's strongest rocket GSLV Mark-3
 phir use chand kii kaksha main pahunchaaya jayega
 Chandrayaan-2 will reach the moon's orbit after about 55 days
 phir lander chand kii sataha par utrega
 After this the rover will come out of it and do various experiments
 chand kii sataha, vaataavaran or mitti kii jaanch karegaa
 At the same time, the orbiter will keep an eye on the lander and rover circling around the moon
 saath hi, rover se mili jaankaree ko isro centre bhejega
 Mission How many days Orbiter - 1 year, Lander (vikram) - 15 days, Rover (pragya) - 15 days Total weight of mission: 3877 kg Orbiter - 2379 kg, Lander (vikram) - 1471 kg, Rover (pragyan) - 27 kg Orbiter: 100 km from Moon
 The isro's mobile command center Chandrayaan-2's orbiter will send the information received from the lander and rover to ISRO center, orbiting 100 km above the moon
 isamen 8 pelod hai
 Also, the command sent from ISRO to the lander and rover
 ise hindustan aironautics limited ne banaakar 2015 main hi isro ko saunp diya tha
 Vikram Lander: ISRO built indigenous Landerlander on Russia's refusal, named after ISRO founder and father of Indian space program Vikram Sarabhai
 isamen 4 pelod hai
 It will carry out scientific experiments for 15 days
 isaki shuruaati dizin isro ke spes aplicoshan centre ahmedabad ne banaaya tha
 Later it was developed by the URSC of Bengaluru
 pragyan roverh is robot ke kandhe par puraa mishan, 15 minute main milegaa data27 kilo ke is robot par hi puure mishan kii jimmdari he
 It has 2 payloads
 chand kii sataha par yah kareeb 400 meter kii duuri tay karegaa
 During this time it will conduct various scientific experiments
 phir chand se praapt jaankaree ko vikram lander par bhejega
 The lander will send data to the orbiter from there
 phir orbitor use isro centre par bhejega
 This entire process will take about 15 minutes
 yani pragyan se bheji gai jaankaree dharti tak aane main 15 minute lagenge
 Why it took 11 years for the launch of Chandrayaan-2 In November 2007, the Russian space agency Rosskosmos said that it would work together in this project
 vah isro ko lander degaa
 In 2008, the mission received approval from the government
 2009 main chandrayan-2 kaa dizin taiyaar kar liya gaya
 The launch was scheduled in January 2013, but the Russian space agency rosscosmos lander could not deliver
 phir isaki lonching 2016 main tay kii gai
 However, in 2015, Rosskosmos withdrew from the project
 phir
 
 
 ISRO made its own indigenous lander, roverissero, decided to launch Chandrayaan-2 in March 2018
 lekin kuch test ke liye lonching ko april 2018 or phir oktober 2018 tak taala gaya
